Architecture\\nThe migration system is orchestrated in `apps/dashboard/pkg/migration/migrate.go`, which defines a singleton `migrator` type that manages the migration pipeline. The main entry point is the `Migrate()` function, which applies frontend defaults, runs sequential schema version migrations (v2 through v42), and performs cleanup.
